[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2882[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mencoding.[0m[1;92mc:2883[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2891[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2883[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Surrogate pair *[0m[35m/[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2884[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mc & [0m[1;36m0xFC00[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0xD800[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2885[0m[39m:                ret = XML_ERR_INTERNAL_ERROR;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2886[0m[39m:                break;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2887[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2888[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39minend - in < [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2889[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        break;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2890[0m[39m:            d = in[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[39m | [0m[1;39m([0m[39min[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m][0m[39m << [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2891[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39md & [0m[1;36m0xFC00[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0xDC00[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Investigate `UTF32ToUTF8`’s contract[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The signature `[0m[1;35mUTF32ToUTF8[0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned char *out, int *outlen, const unsigned [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar *in, int *inlen, void *vctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is designed by the libxml2 encoding API: it [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmust consume up to `*inlen` input bytes, write no more than `*outlen` output bytes,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupdate `*inlen`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`*outlen` to reflect processed/produced counts, and return [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XML_ENC_OK`, `XML_ENC_PARTIAL`, or `XML_ENC_ERR_SPACE`.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Currently, `UTF32ToUTF8` ignores `*outlen`, unconditionally writes [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor each codepoint to `out`, and then stops only on out-of-input or illegal [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msurrogate. This unchecked write leads to a one-byte heap-buffer-overflow when the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer is exactly full.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core fix: introduce output-bounds checks[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - At function start, compute:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       unsigned char *outstart = out;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       unsigned char *outend   = out + [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*outlen[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     so that `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39moutstart, outend[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` bounds contain legal writes.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Before each multi-byte write [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte, [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte, [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte, [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte sequences[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mverify there is enough room:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       - For a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte sequence [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`c < [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m > outend[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break with `ret [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m= XML_ENC_ERR_SPACE;`[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       - For a [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte sequence [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`c < [0m[1;36m0x800[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m > outend[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break similar.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       - For a [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte sequence: if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout + [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m > outend[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       - For a [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte sequence [0m[1;39m([0m[39msurrogate pair[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m > outend[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If we break on insufficient space, the loop ends leaving `ret = [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML_ENC_ERR_SPACE`, then exit. After loop, compute:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       *outlen = out - outstart;    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m actual bytes written[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       *inlen  = in  - instart;     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m actual bytes consumed[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     and return `ret` to signal space shortage.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preserve existing behavior and error signaling[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintain the original logic for detecting invalid surrogate pairs, incomplete [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput, and internal errors, returning existing error codes unchanged.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The return value for partial writes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mspace[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is `XML_ENC_ERR_SPACE`, as [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpected by callers like `xmlEncInputChunk`, ensuring they will grow the buffer and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mretry gracefully.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `encoding.c` at the top of `UTF32ToUTF8`, immediately after current [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariable declarations [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m2850[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      unsigned char *outstart = out;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      unsigned char *outend   = out + [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*outlen[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In the main `[0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[39min < inend[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` conversion loop, before every `out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = …` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mand subsequent `out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, insert an `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout + N > outend[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;` where N [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis the total bytes to be written in that branch.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. After the loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbut before `return ret;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, update:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      *outlen = out - outstart;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      *inlen  = in  - instart;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Remove or defer updating `*outlen` and `*inlen` until after checking bounds; [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure existing update code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is replaced by this unified post-loop update.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Why this approach[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Directly addresses the root cause: unchecked writes in `UTF32ToUTF8`.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Leaves the higher-level encoding routines [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlEncInputChunk`, [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlCharEncInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and parser logic untouched, preserving current functionality, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msince on `XML_ENC_ERR_SPACE`, they will expand buffers and resume conversion.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to fuzz harness or parser code—only the UTF-[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m→UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m conversion [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroutine is hardened.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar patterns already exist in other character conversion routines in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibxml2 [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in UTF16ToUTF8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where they check `out + needed <= outend`.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential side-effects and mitigation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The new checks may slightly reduce throughput on very tight buffers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcorner [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcase[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but correctness is paramount.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Extensive tests or existing fuzz harnesses will now see a correct [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XML_ENC_ERR_SPACE` instead of a crash; any tests relying on silent overflows [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be updated, but none are expected.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: run the full libxml2 test suite and html fuzzing harness to ensure[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno regressions.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The implementation for UTF16ToUTF8 in `encoding.c` already uses an `outend` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguard; model the changes after that pattern.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No modifications to external libraries, fuzz harness, or test code were made.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
